# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Summary

I found all the C++ source files that implement the three core components of the CSS layout engine reflow pipeline in mozilla-firefox/firefox (sg-evals/firefox--871325b8):

### **Frame Construction**
- `layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp/h` - The main frame constructor that converts DOM trees into frame trees

### **Block Layout Reflow**
- `layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.cpp/h` - Implements block frame reflow (nsBlockFrame::Reflow at line 1291)
- `layout/generic/BlockReflowState.cpp/h` - Manages block reflow state and float positioning
- `layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.cpp/h` - Handles reflow of child frames within block contexts

### **Inline Layout Reflow**
- `layout/generic/nsLineLayout.cpp/h` - Manages inline line layout and text wrapping
- `layout/generic/nsLineBox.cpp/h` - Represents and manages individual lines

### **Reflow Infrastructure**
- `layout/generic/ReflowInput.cpp/h` - Carries input parameters for reflow operations
- `layout/generic/ReflowOutput.cpp/h` - Carries reflow results back up the tree

### **Dirty Frame Invalidation** 
- `layout/base/PresShell.cpp/h` - Contains FrameNeedsReflow() which marks frames dirty and schedules reflow (lines 2632-2680)

### **Base Classes**
- `layout/generic/nsIFrame.cpp/h` - Base frame class with virtual Reflow() method
- `layout/generic/nsContainerFrame.cpp/h` - Base class for frames with children
- `layout/generic/nsFloatManager.cpp/h` - Float positioning and available space management

The nsCSSFrameConstructor class is responsible for converting the DOM tree into a frame tree that mirrors the CSS display model. It constructs frames based on CSS display types and handles dynamic updates when content changes. The constructor maintains state about the frame tree and coordinates with the PresShell to schedule reflows when the tree structure changes.\\n\\n**Block Layout Reflow (layout/generic/)**: The block layout reflow mechanism is distributed across several key files:\\n\\n- **nsBlockFrame.cpp/h** implements the main reflow algorithm for block-level and block-equivalent frames.
